## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes v1beta1 to v1 API Storage Version Registration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that register API group storage versions mapping v1beta1 to v1 equivalents. Look for REST storage providers (in pkg/registry/) that define both v1beta1Storage() and v1Storage() methods, the StorageVersion manager interface (in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/), and the ResourceEncodingConfig that controls which GroupVersion is used for etcd storage.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

`validatingadmissionpolicybindings` under `admissionregistration.k8s.io/v1`\\n   - `v1beta1Storage()` registers `validatingadmissionpolicies` and `validatingadmissionpolicybindings` under `admissionregistration.k8s.io/v1beta1`\\n   - Also has `v1alpha1Storage()` for mutating admission policies\\n\\nAdditionally, **`pkg/registry/resource/rest/storage_resource.go`** has `v1beta1Storage()` (for `resource.k8s.io/v1beta1` resources like `deviceclasses`, `resourceclaims`, `resourceclaimtemplates`, `resourceslices`) but no `v1Storage()` \u2014 it pairs with `v1alpha3Storage()` instead.\\n\\n### StorageVersion Manager Interface\\n\\nThe `Manager` interface is defined in **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storageversion/manager.go`** (`sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0`). It provides:\\n- `AddResourceInfo(resources ...*ResourceInfo)` \u2014 records resources whose StorageVersions need updates\\n- `UpdateStorageVersions(kubeAPIServerClientConfig *rest.Config, apiserverID string)` \u2014 updates StorageVersions in the API\\n- `PendingUpdate(gr schema.GroupResource) bool` \u2014 checks if a resource's StorageVersion is still pending\\n- `Completed() bool` \u2014 returns true when all StorageVersion updates are complete\\n\\nThe `ResourceInfo` struct (also in `manager.go`) carries `GroupResource`, `EncodingVersion`, `EquivalentResourceMapper`, `DirectlyDecodableVersions`, and `ServedVersions`.\\n\\nThe default implementation `defaultManager` is created via `NewDefaultManager()` and is stored in `GenericAPIServer.StorageVersionManager` (see `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/genericapiserver.go` and `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/config.go`).\\n\\n### ResourceEncodingConfig \u2014 Controls etcd Storage GroupVersion\\n\\nThe `ResourceEncodingConfig` interface is defined in **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go`** (`sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0`):\\n- `StorageEncodingFor(schema.GroupResource) (schema.GroupVersion, error)` \u2014 returns the serialization format for etcd storage\\n- `InMemoryEncodingFor(schema.GroupResource) (schema.GroupVersion, error)` \u2014 returns the in-memory representation\\n\\nThe concrete implementation `DefaultResourceEncodingConfig` uses a `resources` map of `GroupResource -> OverridingResourceEncoding` to override the default (highest-priority) version for specific resources. The `SetResourceEncoding()` method sets explicit overrides.\\n\\nThe `CompatibilityResourceEncodingConfig` interface adds `BackwardCompatibileStorageEncodingFor()` which uses `emulatedStorageVersion()` to select the appropriate storage version based on the effective Kubernetes version (for version skew compatibility).\\n\\n### How v1beta1 Resources Get Stored as v1 in etcd\\n\\nThe key file is **`pkg/kubeapiserver/default_storage_factory_builder.go`** (`sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0`). The `NewStorageFactoryConfig()` function defines `ResourceEncodingOverrides` \u2014 a list of `schema.GroupVersionResource` entries that specify which resources should be stored in a non-default (typically older) version. For example:\\n- `networking.Resource(\\\"ipaddresses\\\").WithVersion(\\\"v1beta1\\\")` \u2014 stores ipaddresses in v1beta1 instead of the latest v1\\n- `networking.Resource(\\\"servicecidrs\\\").WithVersion(\\\"v1beta1\\\")` \u2014 stores servicecidrs in v1beta1\\n- `storage.Resource(\\\"volumeattributesclasses\\\").WithVersion(\\\"v1beta1\\\")` \u2014 stores volumeattributesclasses in v1beta1\\n\\nThe `completedStorageFactoryConfig.New()` method calls `MergeResourceEncodingConfigs()` (from `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/resourceconfig/helpers.go`) to merge these overrides into the `DefaultResourceEncodingConfig`. The resulting `ResourceEncodingConfig` is embedded in `DefaultStorageFactory` (from `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/storage_factory.go`), which uses it to determine the actual etcd storage version for each GroupResource.\\n\\nFor resources NOT in the override list, the `DefaultResourceEncodingConfig.StorageEncodingFor()` returns the highest-priority registered version (typically v1 for GA resources), meaning v1beta1 API requests are transparently converted to v1 for storage.\"\n}"
